============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK22)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_z*A**c5/(c6*A**c7 + c8)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.2092477763\,A^2\;-\;0.2092477763\,A\,e^{-0.06535116587\,t}\;+\;\frac{0.21528617536\,A^2}{0.97163989983\,A^4+1}.
\]
Key structural facts:
- Depends on \(t\) **only** through the single term \(A e^{kt}\) with \(k=-0.06535...\).
- Has two purely-\(A\) terms: a polynomial \(-0.2092A^2\) and a rational term \(\dfrac{\alpha A^2}{\beta A^4+1}\).
- No logs, tanh, abs, max, etc.

Now check each candidate for whether its form can be tuned (by choosing its free constants) to equal the GT for all \(t,A\).

1) \(A c0/(A+c1)+A c2 e^{c3 t}+c4 e^{c5/(c6+t)}+c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Ac9+1)\).  
Has unavoidable extra \(t\)-dependences (the \(e^{c5/(c6+t)}\) term unless \(c4=0\); and the \(e^{c8 t}\log(\cdot)\) unless \(c7=0\)). Even after zeroing those, remaining \(A c0/(A+c1)\) cannot become \(\alpha A^2/(\beta A^4+1)\) nor \(-0.2092A^2\). No match.

2) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5 + c6 t e^{c7 t}\).  
To match GT, must kill \(t e^{c7 t}\) by \(c6=0\). Also GT has no pure \(A\) linear term \(A c1\) so need \(c1=0\). Then you’d need \(A^{c4}c5\) to represent the rational \(A^2/(A^4+1)\), impossible with a single power. No match.

3) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{A c7 + c8 t}\).  
Must set \(c6=0\) to remove \(e^{A c7}\) dependence. Then still has \(A c1 + A c2\) (must be 0 ⇒ \(c1=c2=0\)). Remaining terms are polynomial in \(A\) plus one separable \(A^{c3}e^{c5 t}\); cannot produce the rational \(A^2/(A^4+1)\). No match.

4) \(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4 t/(c5+t^2)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8 e^{c9|A|}\).  
GT has no \(|A|\) exponential ⇒ need \(c8=0\). Also no \(t/(c5+t^2)\) ⇒ \(c4=0\). Term \(A c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)}\) cannot become \(A e^{kt}\) for all \(t\). No match.

5) \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2 t/(c3+t) + c4\log(A^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}+1)\).  
Need \(c2=0\). Log term cannot be made into rational \(A^2/(A^4+1)\) for all \(A\) (and also introduces \(t\) unless \(c7=0\), then still log). No match.

6) \(A^2c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + A^{c4}c5 e^{c6 t}\log(Ac7+1)+ c8 t/(c9+t)\).  
Need \(c8=0\), \(c3=0\). Log term must vanish ⇒ \(c5=0\) (or \(c7=0\) gives \(\log 1=0\), yes). Then left with \(A^2c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t}\): missing the rational \(A\)-only term. No match.

7) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4 t}\).  
GT has no constant term and no \(e^{c4 t}\) independent of \(A\); must set \(c2=0,c3=0,c1=0\). Leaves only \(A^2c0\), cannot match GT’s additional rational and \(A e^{kt}\) term. No match.

8) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + c2\tanh(c3 t+c4)+ c5|A| + c6 e^{c7 t}/|A|^5\).  
To remove non-GT structures need \(c2=0,c5=0,c6=0,c1=0\). Leaves \(A^2c0\) only. No match.

9) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + A c2\max(0,c3+t)+ A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6)+ c7 t/(c8+t)\).  
Must set \(c2=0,c7=0,c1=0\). Then has \(A^2c0 + A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6)\). The rational here is of form \(\frac{c5 A^{c4}}{A^{c4}+c6}\), which cannot equal \(\frac{\alpha A^2}{\beta A^4+1}\) for all \(A\) (different degrees: denominator power matches numerator power, not \(A^4\) vs \(A^2\)). Also missing \(A e^{kt}\). No match.

10) \(A^5 c0/(c1+t)^5 + A^2c2 + A c3 + c4\tanh(\cdot)+ c7|A|+ c8 e^{c9 t}\).  
Need to kill many terms; even then cannot create \(A e^{kt}\) with correct structure while also producing the specific rational in \(A\). No match.

11) \(A c0/(c1+t) + A c2 + c3 + c4/(c5+t)\).  
GT has exponential in \(t\), not rational in \(t\). No match.

12) \(A c0 e^{c1/(c2+t)} + c3 e^{c4/(c5+t)} + c6\log(c7 e^{A c8}+1)\).  
Wrong \(t\)-dependence (reciprocal shift in exponent), and log-of-exp-in-\(A\). No match.

13) \(A^{c0}c1/(A^{c0}+c2) + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + A^{c6}c7 + c8 t/(c9+t^2)\).

14) \(A c0/(A c1+1) + A^{c2}c3 + A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6) + c7 t e^{c8 t}\).

To get \(A e^{kt}\) you’d need \(|A|^{c9}\) to equal \(A\) for all real \(A\), impossible (absolute value). No match.

16) \(A^2c0 + A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6) + c7 t/(c8+t)\).  
Set \(c7=0\), \(c1=0\). Exponential term can match \(-0.2092 A e^{-0.06535 t}\) by choosing \(c2=-0.2092\), \(c3=-0.06535\). But the rational term is again \(\frac{c5 A^{c4}}{A^{c4}+c6}\), which cannot equal \(\frac{0.2153 A^2}{0.9716 A^4+1}\) for all \(A\). No match.

**GT:** `-0.2092*A² + 0.2153*A²/(0.9716*A⁴ + 1) - 0.2092*A*exp(-0.0654*t)`

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term: `c₀*A²`
2. A rational term: `c₁*A²/(c₂*A⁴ + 1)`
3. An exponential decay term: `c₃*A*exp(-c₄*t)`

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key structural requirements:**
- Must have `A²` term
- Must have `A²/(A⁴ + const)` type rational term (or equivalent)
- Must have `A*exp(negative*t)` term
- No other independent basis functions

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 13:** `A^c0*c1/(A^c0+c2) + A^c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + A^c6*c7 + c8*t/(c9+t²)`

Actually, GT rational term: `0.2153*A²/(0.9716*A⁴+1)`. Can `A^c0/(A^c0+c2)` match `A²/(A⁴+1)`? No, because `A^c0/(A^c0+c2)` has same power in numerator and denominator.

But wait - the full candidate has `A^c0*c1/(A^c0+c2) + A^c6*c7`. Let me think about combining. With c0=4: `c1*A⁴/(A⁴+c2) + c7*A^c6`. Set c6=2: `c1*A⁴/(A⁴+c2) + c7*A²`.

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

- A²: ✓
- A*exp(ct): ✓ (for the exponential decay term)

Hmm, but wait. Can I combine terms? `A²*c0 + c5*A⁴/(A⁴+c6)` = `A²*c0 + c5 - c5*c6/(A⁴+c6)`. GT: `-0.2092*A² + 0.2153*A²/(0.9716*A⁴+1)`. The rational part of GT has A² in numerator, but `-c5*c6/(A⁴+c6)` has no A dependence in numerator. Not equivalent.

What about c4=2? `c5*A²/(A²+c6) + c0*A²`. Let me combine: `c0*A² + c5*A²/(A²+c6)` = `A²(c0 + c5/(A²+c6))` = `A²(c0*A² + c0*c6 + c5)/(A²+c6)`. GT: `A²(-0.2092 + 0.2153/(0.9716*A⁴+1))` = `A²(-0.2092*(0.9716*A⁴+1) + 0.2153)/(0.9716*A⁴+1)` = `A²(-0.2033*A⁴ - 0.2092 + 0.2153)/(0.9716*A⁴+1)` = `A²(-0.2033*A⁴ + 0.0061)/(0.9716*A⁴+1)`.

The candidate gives `A²*(c0*A² + const)/(A²+c6)` - denominator is A²+c6, GT denominator is A⁴+const. Different rational structures.

Also has `c7*t/(c8+t)` and `A*c1` extra terms. Set c1=0, c7=0. Still can't match rational part.
Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 17:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3+1) + A^c4*c5*exp(c6*t)`

**Candidate 24:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2/(A^c1+c3) + A^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*t/(c9+t²)`
- Rational: `A^c1/(A^c1+c3)`. With c1=2: `c2*A²/(A²+c3)`. GT needs `A²/(A⁴+1)`. Different.
- With c1=4: `c2*A⁴/(A⁴+c3)`. Numerator A⁴ not A².

- `c8*t/(c9+t²)`: extra term, set c8=0.
- But still can't get `A²/(A⁴+1)` from `A^c1/(A^c1+c3)`.

Wait, let me reconsider. Can I combine `A*c0 + A^c1*c2/(A^c1+c3)` to get `A²` and `A²/(A⁴+1)`?

With c1=2: `c0*A + c2*A²/(A²+c3)`. I need A² term too. There's no standalone A² term. Set c7 to absorb constant. Hmm, this doesn't have A².

Actually, `c2*A²/(A²+c3) = c2 - c2*c3/(A²+c3)`. So `c0*A + c2 - c2*c3/(A²+c3) + c7`. This gives constant + A term + rational term with no A in numerator. GT needs A² and A²/(A⁴+1). Can't match.

With c1=4: `c0*A + c2*A⁴/(A⁴+c3) + c5*A^c4*exp(c6*t) + c7`. `c2*A⁴/(A⁴+c3) = c2 - c2*c3/(A⁴+c3)`. So I get `c0*A + c2 + c7 - c2*c3/(A⁴+c3) + c5*A*exp(c6*t)`. The rational part is `1/(A⁴+c3)`, not `A²/(A⁴+c3)`. Missing A² in numerator. And no A² polynomial term.
Candidate 24 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 25:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2*exp(A*c3 + c4*t) + c5`
